THE HOLY CHAPEL CHURCH
Holy Chapel Church

(1 John 4:4)

Ye are of God, little childern, and have overcome them: because greater is he that is in you, than he that is in the world.

The Holy Chapel Church(HCC)

was founded in Monrovia, Liberia. The General overseer (most senior pastor) is Kabash A. Cooper, ordained in 1981. The church in America had an average church attendance of 10,000 in 2022.

  1. History
  2. Beliefs
  3. Services




In the presence Of the Lord the is fullness Of Joy

Services

With the special grace of God upon the life of the prophet he speaks in the lives of God's children and begin doing good for the people in the community and around the world.

The Lord has not given us the spirit of fear but the strength to conquer all our fears.


History

The HCC was founded in 1952 by Rev. Kabash A. Cooper (1909â€“1980) following his involvement in other churches. Rev. Melvin Dahn as the next General overseer. Melvin Dahn was a lecturer in mathematics at the University of Liberia, as at the time he joined the church in 1973. He was ordained a pastor of the church in 1975, and his appointment as the leader (General overseer) of the church was formalized by the posthumous reading of Cooper's sealed pronouncement. In 1990, the Holy Chapel Church Bible School was founded. In 1981, Pastor Melvin Dahn became the General Overseer of the Church. In 1983, the land for the Redemption Camp in Bassa was purchased. In 1988, a studentsâ€™ body known as the Holy Chapel Church Fellowship (HCCF) was established. It is the youth wing of the church concentrated within tertiary institutions of learning in the country. In 1990, Christ the Redeemerâ€™s Friends Universal (CRFU), was established to garner financial and human resources from the very wealthy in the society. In 2005, Chapel's University was established. Andrew Rice, writing in The New York Times, calls the HCC "one of [Africa's] most vigorously expansionary religious movements. The church's leaders preach that in the future "In every household, there will be at least one member of Holy Chapel Church in the whole world. In 2008, it had 3,000 churches and 70 thousands members in Liberia, in 9 countries. The international church is structured in different areas throughout the world. The local churches are now grouped into regions, with 10 Regions in Liberia. It is also organised throughout most of the world. Notable special spiritual programs are the Spiritual Renewal Service which holds on the first Week of every month in Liberia. Then, the annual Spiritual Convention (August) and the Spiritual Congress (December) in Liberia and beyond with diverse schedules. In 2020, the Liberia Church had 5,000 people. Our story is an interesting but uncomplicated one when you think about all that God can do and has done for His children. In the year 2020, there was a global pandemic and people were hurting, confused, and upset. Simultaneously, the world was facing a rising civil rights issue, coupled with what turned out to be the largest presidential voting in U.S. history. During this perplexing period in life, God decided to birth something; The Holy Chapel Church.

Birthing The Holy Chapel Church was awesome but the way that God decided to do it was even greater.

We have since learned that the process should be appreciated even when it is puzzling. Our Pastors, Deante and Lesa Lavender, who were the campus managers of The Word Church (Akron Location) were called in to sit with their man of God, Dr. R.A. Vernon. Within minutes of sitting down, Dr. Vernon said â€œI feel God telling me that I should give you the Akron campus to start your church. Youâ€™ve walked with me for years, youâ€™ve walked with them, they are familiar with you, they love you, but most of all you love them. This is your time.â€ â€“ Well thatâ€™s it! No but seriously, at that moment Dr. R.A. Vernon, Dr. Victory Vernon, and the members of The Word Church gave us an unimaginable start and step toward our destiny. Drake said (can you mention Drake on a church siteâ€¦.we will see what happens) â€œStarted from the bottom, now weâ€™re here.â€â€¦that's not our story, but we do know that based on how and where we startedâ€¦we plan on going even further in advancing the message that JESUS IS THE REMEDY!

Beliefs

The official HCC website outlines its beliefs in the Bible and the Holy Trinity, that the Devil exists, that God formed man in his image, in repentance, in cleansing from sins by God's grace, in sanctification, water baptism, Holy Spirit baptism, restitution and that God can heal without medicine (by His divine intervention e.g. through prayer).

Our mission is to spread the love of Jesus Christ and to help individuals find and live in Godâ€™s plan for their lives and to prepare a people for the Lord from all Nations. The people will in turn build the church of the Lord as a kingdom of heaven on earth.

Holy Chapel Church
